9th-32nd Decklists
==================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on June 4, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/hosler.jpg)
By Corbin Hosler











Just outside the Top 8 are the rest of the players who just missed. Many of these decks missed the Top 8 by a hair, and all finished the tournament with a high degree of success. These are the decks that help define the metagame going forward. Here are the decks that finished ninth through 32nd.


Top 32 Decklists  

Corbin Hosler


Just outside the Top 8 are the rest of the players who just missed. Many of these decks missed the Top 8 by a hair, and all finished the tournament with a high degree of success. These are the decks that help define the metagame going forward. Here are the decks that finished ninth through 32nd.







#### Steve Rubin's Black-Green Constrictor – 9th, Grand Prix Omaha


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
